		<div class="left-text"><h2>A Leader in Aesthetic Plastic Surgery</h2></div>

		<section class="content">
			<h2>Your Gateway to Aesthetic Excellence <span class="small">Serving Oakland, Dublin, &amp; the San Francisco Bay Area</span></h2>
<p>If you're looking for a plastic surgeon serving Oakland, Dublin, or the San Francisco Bay area, we are right in your backyard! Tri Valley Plastic Surgery is home to some of the nation's most respected and skilled plastic surgeons. Our surgeons hold leadership positions in national associations and are sought after by patients and fellow surgeons from across the country for their insight and prowess. When you choose Tri Valley Plastic Surgery for your consultation, you are choosing a national leader in plastic surgery.</p>

<div class="mod_doctor_feature viewport container" data-s3-module>
	<div class="row ">
		<div class="content">
			<div class="title">
				<h2>Dr. Steven <span class="block-desktop">Williams</span> <span class="small">Leader and Trailblazer in Medical Aesthetics</span></h2>
			</div>
			<div class="box-copy">
				<p>Dr. Williams is a board-certified plastic and reconstructive surgeon and a diplomate of the <a href="https://www.abplasticsurgery.org/">American Board of Plastic Surgery</a>. With over a decade of experience and training at Yale University School of Medicine, you can rest assured you are getting more than just the standard of care - you are getting the epitome of care. Dr. Williams formerly served as the President of the prestigious <a href="https://www.plasticsurgery.org/">American Society of Plastic Surgeons</a>. Dr. Williams has held multiple leadership roles over the years, including various committee chairs and Vice President for Aesthetic Surgery. In this capacity, Dr. Williams acted as a leader among leaders, guiding best practices for plastic surgeons across the nation.</p>
			</div>
		</div>

        <div class="copy padded">
            <div class="inner">
                                <div class="content" data-api-key="content">
                    <h2>Past President of ASPS <span class="small">Dr. Steven Williams is honored to have been elected the President of the American Society of Plastic Surgeons</span></h2>
<p>As a board-certified plastic and reconstructive surgeon who has spent his career remaining committed to helping patients live their ideal lives, as the leader of an organization that represents more than 7,000 physicians, Dr. Williams&rsquo; expertise and commitment to excellence will help to guide the next generation of cosmetic surgeons.</p>
<p>Dr. Williams is honored to have served as the first-ever African American president of what is now the largest and most prominent plastic surgery organization in the world and can&rsquo;t wait to put his decades of experience to use, shaping the future of cosmetic surgery.</p>
<p><a href="/about/asps-past-president-steven-williams/" class="btn">Read More about Dr. Williams</a></p>
